# Patrick Hwu, MD
![Patrick  Hwu](https://www.moffitt.org/globalassets/images/researchers_bio/HwuPatrick_27923.jpg)
Patrick Hwu, MD 
CEO
**Program:** Cutaneous Oncology 
**Research Program:** Immuno-Oncology Program 
[Google Scholar Profile](https://scholar.google.com/citations?user=wLSQt98AAAAJ&hl=en)
[ Contact ](https://eforms.moffitt.org/ContactResearchersForm?PERID=27923)
  * ## Overview
Dr. Hwu has a proven track record leading collaborative teams to make breakthroughs in science while improving cancer outcomes for cancer patients.
### Associations
    * Cutaneous Oncology
    * Immuno-Oncology Program
### Education & Training
**Board Certification:**
    * Medical Oncology - Medical Oncology
**Fellowship:**
    * National Cancer Institute - Medical Oncology and Immunology
**Residency:**
    * Johns Hopkins Hospital - Internal Medicine
**Medical School:**
    * Medical College of Pennsylvania - MD
  * ## Research Interest
Known for leading transformative research into the clinic, Hwu helped pioneer the field of gene modified T cells, publishing research on the first chimeric antigen receptor directed against cancer. His work focuses on vaccines, adoptive T-cell therapies and immune resistance. He is the principal investigator on a National Institutes of Health SPORE grant for melanoma and has more than 270 peer-reviewed publications. An internationally recognized physician scientist, Hwu has a proven track record leading collaborative teams to make breakthroughs in science while improving cancer outcomes for cancer patients.
